	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('C'))
		++residue_ATTTAC;
	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('G'))
		++residue_ATTTAG;
	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('T'))
		++residue_ATTTAT;

	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('C') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('A'))
		++residue_ATTTCA;
	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('C') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('C'))
		++residue_ATTTCC;
	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('C') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('G'))
		++residue_ATTTCG;

		++residue_ATTTCT;

	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('G') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('A'))
		++residue_ATTTGA;
	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('G') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('C'))
		++residue_ATTTGC;
	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('G') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('G'))
		++residue_ATTTGG;
	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('G') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('T'))
		++residue_ATTTGT;

	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('A'))
		++residue_ATTTTA;
	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('C'))
		++residue_ATTTTC;

		++residue_ATTTTG;
	else if (in_dna_2[i]->Equals('A') && in_dna_2[i+1]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+2]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+3]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+4]->Equals('T') && in_dna_2[i+5]->Equals('T'))
		++residue_ATTTTT;
